			tailZone = new org.joda.time.tz.DateTimeZoneBuilder.DSTZone(tailZone.getID() , tailZone.iStandardOffset , tailZone.iStartRecurrence , tailZone.iEndRecurrence.renameAppend("-Summer"));
		}
	} 
}
